{"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_1","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"sed -n '1,240p' /app/RELIQUARY.md\"","aggregated_output":"# Reliquary command reference\n\nCoordinates are `(row,column)`, with `(0,0)` at the northwest. A direction used for movement is one of `north`, `south`, `east`, or `west`. A turn is `clockwise` or `counterclockwise`. Dials use the orientation cycle `N,E,S,W`.\n\nInvoke one command per process, such as `/app/reliquary status`. State is retained between invocations.\n\n- `look`: show the entire known 7x7 floor. This is a free observation.\n- `status`: show exact player, crate, dial, gate, inventory, reset, and seal state. This is a free observation.\n- `help`: show a short command reminder. This is a free observation.\n- `new`: restore the investigative session. This meta-command cannot appear in a solution.\n- `move D`: move one tile. If the player enters ice, it keeps moving in `D` through consecutive passable cells until it reaches a non-ice tile or is blocked.\n- `push C D`: while immediately behind crate `C`, push it one tile in `D`. Amber accepts only east/west pushes and jade only north/south pushes. A pushed crate slides like the player. A push can be legal and still be irreversible.\n- `turn X T`: while on or orthogonally adjacent to dial `X`, rotate it one quarter-turn. `seal` is also turnable once it is armed at the reliquary.\n- `take I`: take item `I` from the player's tile during the item phase.\n- `drop I`: drop a carried item on the player's tile during the item phase.\n- `use reset shrine`: while on the reset shrine, spend its one use. Inventory and player position remain unchanged; crates move to their marked reset positions, plate occupancy is recomputed, and seal progress is cleared.\n- `use sun reliquary`: while on the reliquary, consume the sun key and arm the seal. All four dials must have their etched target orientations and the reset must have been used.\n- `wait`: perform no primary movement, but still run conveyors, plates, gates, and terminal checks.\n\nAfter any puzzle command, every crate already resting on a lettered conveyor moves at most one cell in that dial's current orientation. Conveyor movement does not trigger ice sliding until some later primary movement enters ice. Crates block players and one another.\n\nThe amber plate is a hold plate: gate A is open only while amber remains on it. The jade plate is latched: jade's first arrival permanently opens gate B. The reset recomputes the hold plate but does not undo a latch already set.\n\nOnce armed, the four-input seal sequence is read from the final orientations in alphabetical dial order. Enter `clockwise` for `N` or `E`, and `counterclockwise` for `S` or `W`. A wrong input is legal but clears seal progress.\n\nMap symbols:\n\n```text\n@ player       A amber crate    J jade crate      k sun key\na/b/g/d dial   ~ ice            x reset shrine    R reliquary\n> < ^ v conveyor (current direction)              p empty plate\nP occupied plate                # wall/closed gate / open gate\n. floor\n```\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
